TL/DL: I will buy this game, if there's NO DLC and/or SEASON PASS.  Except... Check the "Con section"   First impression -   Pros:  1. Like Marvel Vs Capcom back in the days, air combos is fun to play, and fun to watch = Perfect for streaming and e-sport viewership. 2. Knock each other out of the wall into other scene, fresh & nice change of scenary. 3. 4v4 instead of 3v3, like #2, fresh, and potential. 4. Arc System = Good fighting game DNA, reputation worthy of people's initial attention. 5. Animation is Japanese style = fun, nice, and stylish (Storm's facial expression looks more than hot & attractive, much like a warrior lady-like, similar to the first wonder woman movie impression.) 6. Like #5, Marvel girl's Voice Acting especially... VA makes the characters more lovable  Now, POTENTIAL CONs.  1. Temptation to ***SEASON PASS***, there are a lot of characters from Marvel, keep it a handy 50-60 for 4v4, and that's it. Reasoning: a) Balancing! (This ruined Dead or Alive Series) b) Feeling of never ending Money grab. c) You are actually stopping new entry gamers to joining into this game.  2. From trailer, only 8 characters, so BALANCE of involved characters is important, as rough estimate, 50-60 should be a decent number for 4v4 format. (Under the context that every characters is well balanced and/or counter-able to each other.)  ****SUGGESSTIONS*****  I want to buy this game, I want to see it bring back the glory of Marvel Vs. Capcom 2, for decade long glory. So here are my suggestions as an unprofessional gamer/viewer.  1. I know you need to make money, and the current fighting game is not as crazy as MOBA games, I get it. That's why the more reason for you to refrain from DLC, use this game for a good FOUNDATION for the genre.  2. For making money, try focus on making SKINS, like Dead or alive.   DLC SKIN only is good to attract players to spend more money or stay with game, and it does not affect BALACING When you DLC heros, you face problems with: a) Balacing: extra resource requirement from development team b) Discouraging new players to purchase title: People doesn't have enough money to buy a "FULL GAME" + "Required DLC" just to start a game/genre which will make them lose a lot to begin with.  3) When you really really have to DLC characters, keep it OUT of Marvel, aka external collaboration; it's good for everyone: a) Justify for the extra price tag. b) Use each "Collaboration" as a version benchmark, good to avoid balancing issues and still attracts new players to join THIS GAME.  4) If you look at Tekken, Street Fighters...etc, sure they have a lot of season pass and dlc, but that's because: a) Players doesn't have much choice b) Those dev. team are in the "GAME" for decades, they are the leading giants, and they make the rules.  So if you want to CONVINCE PLAYERS to divert their time and money to YOU, try to do it a more sincere and old-school way: GIVE THE PLAYERS THE ACTUAL FULL GAME with ONLY ONE PRICE TAG.  Charge us $80 or $90, but don't do different versions, DLCs, Season Passes. You are Marvel Empire that can afford to pay an actor/actress 10+ Millions for a movie, surely you have the resources to sell a "FULL GAME" like developers back in the days?  ...I sure hope so, otherwise, I rather play MOBA, at least new players keeps coming into the communities.  Have a nice day people.

Takes around 6 more years, removes 6 bad less popular legacy Marvel chars and replace with new ones. They have to make 36 new chars in those 6 years. Then release it as MVC5.
